  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_90da9d66-a9d2-4507-961f-b528aeed99ab'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer10527905223739617367">I'm not your typical girl. I've been running away from the memories that haunt me for so long that depression has become my only comfort.   <span id="freeText10527905223739617367" style="display:none">I'm not your typical girl. I've been running away from the memories that haunt me for so long that depression has become my only comfort. I was content in the darkness...until Wes Michals offered to be my light.<br /><br />I didn't know that time wasn't my ally -- that every second that ticked past was one step closer to the end of something that was beginning to mean the end of myself. He tried to warn me. He promised me all he was able to offer--each moment as it came--but it would never be enough.<br /><br />Sometimes when you think it's the end, it's only the beginning. Wes thought he could save me, but in giving me everything, he ruined me. Because after one kiss, one touch, I couldn't--I wouldn't ever be the same.<br /><br />And from that moment on, his heartbeat became my own.</span>

<div id="review_693084111" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/693084111" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/693084111?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer693084111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2794790657170155155"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383434219i/6555261._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Casting for Wes & Kiersten:<br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432814i/870579.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> 4.5 stars </b> ** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br/><br/><b><em>Ruin</em> made me laugh, cry and swoon. If you want a book that will both leave you uplifted and make you smile while still having a lot of emotional depth, then pick this one up and fall in love with Wes Michels. But bring tissues! It's a tearjerker! </b><br/><br/>This is the story of a sweet, innocent, small-town girl, lost in hurt and reeling from a tragic loss, and a cocky but charming boy, who understood her pain and could reach through to her</span>
  <span id="freeText2794790657170155155" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383434219i/6555261._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Casting for Wes &amp; Kiersten:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432814i/870579.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 4.5 stars </b> ** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br><br><b><em>Ruin</em> made me laugh, cry and swoon. If you want a book that will both leave you uplifted and make you smile while still having a lot of emotional depth, then pick this one up and fall in love with Wes Michels. But bring tissues! It's a tearjerker! </b><br><br>This is the story of a sweet, innocent, small-town girl, lost in hurt and reeling from a tragic loss, and a cocky but charming boy, who understood her pain and could reach through to her because he too had deep painful secrets that made him value every moment of life.<br><br>This book is really hard to describe without spoilers so I'm going to stay very vague about it and say only this: you find something out about the hero very early on and yes, your suspicions are going to be right. Just hold on to the fact that there's a HEA and you'll get through it just fine. It's totally worth the journey.<br><br>Despite the fact that the emotional undercurrents of this story are quite heartbreaking, the majority of the book made me laugh and smile and just feel <em>good</em>. I'll give you an example that's close to the beginning of the book. This is their first meeting:<br><blockquote>
  <em>"I turned around… and ran smack dab into a tree.</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>Or at least it felt like a tree.</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>But trees weren't warm.</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>And they didn't have one, two, three, four, six, Good Lord, eight? Eight packs? Furthermore, had I actually been feeling said person's eight pack? And, dear God, I was counting. I had touched each muscle. And great, my hand was still firmly placed against the guy's stomach. </em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>I jerked my hand back and closed my eyes.</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>"Were you just counting my abs?"</em>
</blockquote><br>Wes was the kind of hero who it was impossible not to fall in love with. What a total sweetheart! He had a wisdom that came out of surviving painful heartbreak, and a protective caring side that just made me swoon for pages on end. I'm smiling here just thinking about him. The things he <em>said </em>melted my heart over and over again.<br><blockquote>
  <em>"I can tell you have a good heart… because the minute I met you, I wanted to fight for it."</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>She was silent.</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>"That's how you can tell when someone has a good heart… when you want to be the one to make it beat."</em>
</blockquote><br>Kiersten was a little more 'innocent' than I'd usually like but at the same time, she didn't let anyone walk all over her and certainly wasn't stupid and so given her history, I could understand where she was coming from. She was hiding a lot of pain though behind her smiles and Wes was just the right kind of guy to help her through it.<br><blockquote>
  <em>"Open." He nipped at the corner of my mouth. "I won't hurt you."</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>"I don't bite."</em>
  <br>
  <em>"But you do lick."</em>
  <br>
  <em>"Always."</em>
</blockquote><br>The writing was awesome! Their banter back and forth was just gold! Fast, snappy, fun, flirty. But it was their deeper connection that really made me <em>care</em>. He chased away her nightmares, made her smile again and taught her to live.<br><blockquote>
  <em>"My new job description is making you laugh and chasing away the bad dreams."</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>"Just because you need help to cope doesn't make you any less strong. The truly weak people in this life are the ones who can't admit they need help. They're the ones who can't admit that they can no longer go at it alone. Those are the people who are weak. By asking for help, by taking help, you've just admitted your weakness and in that, you find your strength. The weak of the world are those who think they've got it all figured out and flaunt it to others."</em>
</blockquote><br>Now because of the 'situation', Wes refused to let her fall in love with him at first. But at the same time, couldn't stay away.<br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I was keeping something epic from her, which sort of made me the villain in this tale. But damn, I wanted to be the hero."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The side characters in this book were equally wonderful. I loooooved Gabe! He was kind of a protective big brother character to Kiersten and the way he mother henned her was endearing and totally hilarious! I really hope he gets his own book! I'd love to see him in the hero role!<br><br>The ending kind of snuck up on me. It wasn't a 'surprise' per say because we knew what was going on from very early on in the book but I guess I was so caught up with them falling in love that it just hit me in the face a little and I read the last 20% of the book quite choked up. And, this might sound weird though but I didn't cry until a certain reveal very close to the end but when I read it, just BAM. Tears. Full body shivers. It was such a beautiful little twist. I loved it.<br><br>The book leaves you with a wonderful message to appreciate every moment of life. It's an uplifting ending. One that gives you hope.<br><blockquote>
  <em>"I want all of [your heart], even the broken pieces, the shredded ones that no longer fit. I want all of them - all of you. I need it all."</em>
</blockquote><br>This really is a very swoony book. Almost no angst, and no stupidity or eye-roll inducing moments. There were times when I found it a little too 'perfect' but at the same time, with all the gritty and 'real' books I've been reading lately, this was exactly what I wanted. I think the point of it was to be uplifting. Miracles <em>do </em>happen. And sometimes, you do get a second chance.<br><br>I loved <em>Ruin</em> and would definitely recommend it.<br><br>This is a standalone romance with a HEA (and epilogue).<br><br>4.5 stars.<br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2794790657170155155" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_692636346" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692636346" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692636346?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692636346" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3183557829808221758"><b>4-4.5 ‘Do it afraid’ stars!</b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/1B78568A-1741-4DB8-AFAD-0ED37ED1E559_zpspmidfyqe.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445691991i/16692273._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 1B78568A-1741-4DB8-AFAD-0ED37ED1E559_zpspmidfyqe.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> “You rescued me and I found my ruin. I’m ruined for you- and I won’t ever be the same. It’s the greatest gift anyone’s ever given me.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br/><i>Ruin</i> is an emotional, raw and beautiful love story that was equal parts heartbreaking and heartwarming. I laughed, I cried, I loved, I smiled. Overall, a very good read. <br/><br/>Wes- aka Wolf- is one of those heroes you find yourself loving straight away. He’s sweet, funny, charming and just a wee bit cocky. He’s a big shot f</span>
  <span id="freeText3183557829808221758" style="display:none"><b>4-4.5 ‘Do it afraid’ stars!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/1B78568A-1741-4DB8-AFAD-0ED37ED1E559_zpspmidfyqe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445691991i/16692273._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1B78568A-1741-4DB8-AFAD-0ED37ED1E559_zpspmidfyqe.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> “You rescued me and I found my ruin. I’m ruined for you- and I won’t ever be the same. It’s the greatest gift anyone’s ever given me.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><i>Ruin</i> is an emotional, raw and beautiful love story that was equal parts heartbreaking and heartwarming. I laughed, I cried, I loved, I smiled. Overall, a very good read. <br><br>Wes- aka Wolf- is one of those heroes you find yourself loving straight away. He’s sweet, funny, charming and just a wee bit cocky. He’s a big shot football player and well known on campus. He’s also a RA at a freshman dorm. He runs into Kiersten and is instantly drawn to her. There is something different about her. She’s innocent, kind, and he can tell she’s holding on to some sort of pain. Due to her innocent nature, he starts calling her Lamb. The Wolf and Lamb nick names were too cute. <br><br>Wes has a secret. A secret we readers find out early on. As Wes and Kiersten’s relationship moves forward, I wanted him to tell her so badly. But I understood why he didn’t. Kiersten has baggage and a past and Wes is focused on helping her move forward and really live her life. Their story was beautiful. <br><i>
  <blockquote> “I can tell you have a good heart… because the minute I met you, I wanted to fight for it.” </blockquote>
</i><br>I don’t want to talk too much about the story because this is one of those books that could be very easily spoiled. I did however love the ending. It’s one of those books that have been out for a while and I keep asking myself why did I wait so long to read it??? I enjoyed the story, Wes and Kiersten were fantastic and GABE was a wonderful side character! I can’t wait to read his story next! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%208/E9BDD035-AD8C-43AF-8A9B-EA3C52FA88DF_zpsranpbzg3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445691991i/16692274._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo E9BDD035-AD8C-43AF-8A9B-EA3C52FA88DF_zpsranpbzg3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>P.S. I listened to the audio book of <i>Ruin</i>… this is one of those times I wish I would have quit the audio and switched to reading. The male narration was terrible. It sounded like Kiersten was a college freshman (as it should) and Wes was a 50 year old creeper. His voice did not match the character at all. Just a heads up for my audible peeps. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3183557829808221758" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_693054616" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/693054616" />
    <a title="MK~ Picky Girl " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9937768-mk-picky-girl"><img alt="MK~ Picky Girl " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386097528p2/9937768.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/693054616?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MK~ Picky Girl " class="user" itemprop="url" name="MK~ Picky Girl " href="/user/show/9937768-mk-picky-girl">MK~ Picky Girl </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer693054616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1009909697218716492"><blockquote> <a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/Ho%20hum/golferbill48/Bored.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432810i/870567.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> </blockquote><br/><br/>See that picture above, that is how I felt while reading Ruin. Unfortunately, I was bored!! It was just too "sugary sweet" for me. <br/><br/> I really don't have a ton to say about the novel Ruin. I'm probably one of the few people out there that thought this book was just ok.. It's a storyline that I have encountered before, many times in fact. It wasn't bad per say but it certainly wasn't amazing. I'm having a hard time trying to figure out why it got so many five star reviews. <br/><br/>Here are my issues: <br/>The</span>
  <span id="freeText1009909697218716492" style="display:none"><blockquote> <a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/Ho%20hum/golferbill48/Bored.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432810i/870567.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </blockquote><br><br>See that picture above, that is how I felt while reading Ruin. Unfortunately, I was bored!! It was just too "sugary sweet" for me. <br><br> I really don't have a ton to say about the novel Ruin. I'm probably one of the few people out there that thought this book was just ok.. It's a storyline that I have encountered before, many times in fact. It wasn't bad per say but it certainly wasn't amazing. I'm having a hard time trying to figure out why it got so many five star reviews. <br><br>Here are my issues: <br>The love connection between Kiersten and Wes felt rushed, sort of like insta love to me. It just wasn't believable. I couldn't buy into their rushed relationship in spite of Wes' circumstances. <br><br> Kiersten's issues with her parents were only briefly touched upon. I wanted more dialogue regarding her hangups and insecurities. <br><br>I did love the message of the story, " living life to it's fullest" but I think the execution is lacking a bit. I needed more dialogue, more plot, more story. <br><br>2 stars from this very picky book snob. <br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b> Buddy read with my girls!!! <a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/Destiny%27s%20child%20gif/L-a-d-y-L-i-k-e/Graphics/soldier.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432810ra/870568.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1009909697218716492" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_667743147" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Jess-i-ca ~Sometimes a Gif Witch~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8740772-jess-i-ca-sometimes-a-gif-witch"><img alt="Jess-i-ca ~Sometimes a Gif Witch~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487382075p2/8740772.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer667743147" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13171516880368754237"><br/>Really enjoyed this one even though it wasn't realistic..Did a lot of<br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_lo7lzeaJFF1qlt9puo1_r1_500_zps42d122ea.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>and<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429196ra/859538.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>and<br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tantrum_zps546d7cd8.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429196ra/859539.gif' alt='not fair photo tantrum_zps546d7cd8.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Kiersten is struggling with her parents death. She finally decides to get out and try to embrace life. She meets the RA at her college, Wes. Their nicknames for each other were cute. (Kiersten - Lamb, Weston - Wolf)<br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_m3nbl4vQUc1rt7c04o1_500_zps13f5065c.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429196ra/859540.gif' alt='my man photo tumblr_m3nbl4vQUc1rt7c04o1_500_zps13f5065c.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Weston is sick (but still HOT!). He doesn't know if he will live or die (Not a spoiler b/c you find this out pretty fast something is wrong) He starts falling for Kiersten and wants to live for her.</span>
  <span id="freeText13171516880368754237" style="display:none"><br>Really enjoyed this one even though it wasn't realistic..Did a lot of<br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_lo7lzeaJFF1qlt9puo1_r1_500_zps42d122ea.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429196ra/859537.gif" alt="crying photo tumblr_lo7lzeaJFF1qlt9puo1_r1_500_zps42d122ea.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429196ra/859538.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tantrum_zps546d7cd8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429196ra/859539.gif" alt="not fair photo tantrum_zps546d7cd8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kiersten is struggling with her parents death. She finally decides to get out and try to embrace life. She meets the RA at her college, Wes. Their nicknames for each other were cute. (Kiersten - Lamb, Weston - Wolf)<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_m3nbl4vQUc1rt7c04o1_500_zps13f5065c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429196ra/859540.gif" alt="my man photo tumblr_m3nbl4vQUc1rt7c04o1_500_zps13f5065c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Weston is sick (but still HOT!). He doesn't know if he will live or die (Not a spoiler b/c you find this out pretty fast something is wrong) He starts falling for Kiersten and wants to live for her.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/9072385_zps5d02c734.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429196i/859541._SY540_.jpg" alt="hotguy photo 9072385_zps5d02c734.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kiersten finds out he is sick and doesn't want to lose another person in her life. She has to be the strong one for him.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_mkfv6vxJ7u1s1terdo1_500_zpsc442f886.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412963ra/812472.gif" alt="love you photo tumblr_mkfv6vxJ7u1s1terdo1_500_zpsc442f886.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i><b><u>Favorite Quotes </u><br><br>"I hated God for taking everyone from me. I hated that in the end, I would always be alone to mourn the loss of the ones I loved."<br><br>"Living is hard - dying is easy. You close your eyes and neve ropen them up again. What's so difficult about that? Nothing really - except it hurts like hell to those you leave behind."<br><br>"She has absolutely no idea what she does to me..She's my medicine, my cure, my everything. If only hearts could heal that way - through someone else's beating."</b><br><br><br>Just a thought- Gabe was like the Gay BFF but he wasn't gay....I think he needs his own book :)</i></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/695288405" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/695288405?book_show_action=true">Aug 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer695288405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10572513789827991452"><b>
  <i>"Fear can be your ally. You can do something afraid."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433121i/871401._SX540_.jpg' width='401' height='375' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Fair is fair, I didn’t care for this author’s previous book and did a review stating all the things that made it an unbearable read for me. <br/><br/>My how the tide has changed…<br/><br/>I found this book to be ABSOLUTELY FANTASTIC, MIRACULOUS, HILARIOUS, SWOON WORTHY, HEART BREAKING and it more than deserves my 5 stars. <br/><br/>This story is told in the dual pov of college freshman, Kiersten Rowe and senior/quarterback/son of one of the world's richest man, Wes Mic</span>
  <span id="freeText10572513789827991452" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Fear can be your ally. You can do something afraid."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433121i/871401._SX540_.jpg" width="401" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fair is fair, I didn’t care for this author’s previous book and did a review stating all the things that made it an unbearable read for me. <br><br>My how the tide has changed…<br><br>I found this book to be ABSOLUTELY FANTASTIC, MIRACULOUS, HILARIOUS, SWOON WORTHY, HEART BREAKING and it more than deserves my 5 stars. <br><br>This story is told in the dual pov of college freshman, Kiersten Rowe and senior/quarterback/son of one of the world's richest man, Wes Michals. All supporting characters were just as strong as the main characters in this story.<br><br>Kiersten grows beyond her fears and smothering depression. While Wes faces his morality through witty banter, grand gestures and friendship they face their future and they build a relationship that book couples are celebrated for. <br><br>This is a love story, a story of friendship, of fears, of trust and of forevers. What more could a reader ask for? Some had said the story is unrealistic but my good read friends, miracles happen every day. <br><br><b>
  <i>"She has absolutely no idea what she does to me..She's my medicine, my cure, my everything. If only hearts could heal that way - through someone else's beating."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“I can tell you have a good heart…” I sighed, opening the door to the outside. “…because the minute I met you, I wanted to fight for it.” She was silent. “That’s how you can tell when someone has a good heart.” </i>
</b><br><br>Happy tears streamed down this readers face while I read, as well as real laugh out loud moments. I just loved every second of this journey and I already feel like going back to page 1 and doing it all over again. <br><br>P.S. I would love for Gabe to receive his own book….please!<br><br><b>
  <i>”You rescued me and I found my ruin.” I bit down on my lip. “I’m ruined for you – and I won’t ever be the same. It’s the greatest gift anyone’s ever given me.”</i>
</b><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1734588536" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1734588536" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1734588536?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who love emotional pain.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=family-friendship">family-friendship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1734588536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1766143812390500649"><br/><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 of 3 from Ruin series<br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471950836i/20128892.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Weston (Wes) Michels was a star quarterback senior. He acquired celebrity status with his good looks and family wealth. He could get any girl he wanted but that didn't concern him because he had a personal quest to fulfill. And the person that caught his attention happened to be a timid freshman.<br/><br/>Kiersten Rowe had been living in the shadows since her life was turned upside down by a tragedy. L</span>
  <span id="freeText1766143812390500649" style="display:none"><br><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 of 3 from Ruin series<br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471950836i/20128892.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Weston (Wes) Michels was a star quarterback senior. He acquired celebrity status with his good looks and family wealth. He could get any girl he wanted but that didn't concern him because he had a personal quest to fulfill. And the person that caught his attention happened to be a timid freshman.<br><br>Kiersten Rowe had been living in the shadows since her life was turned upside down by a tragedy. Life for her was simply breathing for another day. That was until Wes immersed himself into her life and help her live it as she should. But sometimes in life, just as the sun emerged, a dark cloud threatened to darken the day.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I keep seeing this book under various sad book lists and have been wanting to read it for a while. I'm glad I finally took the plunge because it was worth the pain lol!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>I told her I wanted her world to change. Hadn’t expected mine to shift as well.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Wes was very easy to love. I don't just mean his physical appearance but also his heart. For someone in his position, you would think he'd be an ass, but it was far from it. And the things that came out from his mouth could make anyone either weak in the knees or bawl their eyes out.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471950836i/20128893.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've always love characters with emotional darkness. Kiersten had it but I do wish I could see it more distinctively. I love how she had a great support system among her friends.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>"Nobody is promised anything. That’s why life’s so precious.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love seeing selflessness in characters and this book had several of them. The interactions between main characters and the secondary characters gave this book extra heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>I wanted more. But people didn’t always get what they wanted.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love the book overall, but I didn't really like the ending. After all that happened if felt a little cop out. I understand such situation could happen, but it was too much, too soon for me. I would have prefer it turned out differently or at least make it more gradually.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“You rescued me and I found my ruin.” I bit down on my lip. “I’m ruined for you — and I won’t ever be the same. It’s the greatest gift anyone’s ever given me.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ruin is a story of a couple turning on a new leaf and living their life on their own time. It's sad yet heartwarming and reminds us sometimes things happened for a reason.<br><br><i><b>Note 1:</b> <br>Before I started this book, I didn't intend to read the rest of the series. But I love Gabe so much, I need to know his story. Damn. Lol!<br><br><b>Note 2: </b><br>The red text in the teaser background is her “Ways To Live” list</i><br><br><br><b>Books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18134249.Ruin__Ruin___1_" title="Ruin (Ruin, #1) by Rachel Van Dyken" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1374686324s/18134249.jpg" alt="Ruin (Ruin, #1) by Rachel Van Dyken" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18935386.Toxic__Ruin___2_" title="Toxic (Ruin, #2) by Rachel Van Dyken" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1392568117s/18935386.jpg" alt="Toxic (Ruin, #2) by Rachel Van Dyken" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20750028.Fearless__Ruin___2_5_" title="Fearless (Ruin, #2.5) by Rachel Van Dyken" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1391819489s/20750028.jpg" alt="Fearless (Ruin, #2.5) by Rachel Van Dyken" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20800343.Shame__Ruin___3_" title="Shame (Ruin, #3) by Rachel Van Dyken" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1409163261s/20800343.jpg" alt="Shame (Ruin, #3) by Rachel Van Dyken" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454304059i/17942101.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=meli-s-top-favourites">meli-s-top-favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer696131467" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17621525054287613429"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 'RUINED ME' STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433241ra/871723.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>She has absolutely no idea what she does to me.... She’s my medicine, my cure, my everything. If only hearts could heal that way – through someone else’s beating.<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Well, when I decided to read this book, I was <b>NOT</b> expecting to read what I read. I <b>thought</b> it would be your typical bad boy story, but it was so much <b>more</b>. I am <b>SO</b> glad I gave this a try. I don</span>
  <span id="freeText17621525054287613429" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 'RUINED ME' STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433241ra/871723.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>She has absolutely no idea what she does to me.... She’s my medicine, my cure, my everything. If only hearts could heal that way – through someone else’s beating.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Well, when I decided to read this book, I was <b>NOT</b> expecting to read what I read. I <b>thought</b> it would be your typical bad boy story, but it was so much <b>more</b>. I am <b>SO</b> glad I gave this a try. I don't think this review will be very long. I <b>DON'T</b> want to give anything away. It's one of those books that you should just read <b>without</b> finding out too much about it. It might <b>ruin</b> the whole story for you and that would be a <b>shame</b>, because it's a <b>beautiful</b> one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433241i/871724._SY540_.png" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>I looked into his eyes and knew, this was the guy – he was the one I wanted to spend my every waking moment with. He was my forever. <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Kiersten Rowe</b> has had a <b>terrible</b> event happen in her past. And this event is what is keeping her from <b>overcoming</b> her fears. She still feels the <b>pain</b> of her <b>loss</b> and is barely living her <b>life</b>. She is an innocent <b>"lamb"</b> and a sweet girl. But that didn't mean she couldn't <b>stand up</b> for herself. She was quite <b>strong</b> too. Then she meets the boy with the <b>bad</b> reputation and gorgeous smile. She finds her <b>boundaries</b> being pushed, her <b>protective</b> shield lowering, and being <b>taught</b> life lessons. She is also falling <b>in love</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433241i/871725.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I can tell you have a good heart..." I sighed, opening the door to the outside. "...because the minute I met you, I wanted to fight for it."<br><br>"When you want to start a war?" She laughed, clearly trying to lighten my mood.<br><br>"Nah" I sighed. "When you want to be the one to make it beat."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Weston Michels</b> is the school's <b>"bad wolf"</b> football star with a <b>big</b> secret. Only those few <b>really</b> close to him know the <b>truth</b>. When he meets the beautiful freshman, he <b>never</b> thought that this girl would <b>change</b> him forever. I don't think I have ever <b>SWOONED</b> so hard for a character, I couldn't stop melting and smiling for him. I was <b>falling</b> in <b>love</b> with him right along with Kiersten, I mean it's <b>really</b> hard not to. He was full of <b>wisdom</b> that helped Kiersten. And Kiersten gave him a reason to <b>fight</b> his ordeal.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445490372ra/16660472.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though this book was quite <b>sad</b>, it never became <b>too</b> much that it <b>depressed</b> you. There were a lot of <b>funny, sweet,</b> and <b>happy</b> moments. I <b>loved</b> how they met! Then there are the secondary characters, all of which were <b>awesome</b>. Her uncle was the <b>best</b>. Wes's dad was <b>really</b> great as well. Lisa was <b>humourous</b> and <b>loud</b>. And <b>Gabe</b>, I wish I could <b>have</b> him for a best friend, hell I'd <b>want</b> more with him. He stole a piece of my <b>heart</b> and I really wish <b>his</b> story would be told in a <b>future</b> book. He was Kiersten's <b>protector</b> and he was so freaking <b>hilarious</b>. I <b>loved</b> him!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>Gabe held my face between his hands. “What you two have --it’s a once in a lifetime-- you fight for him, sweetheart. Fight for him with every last breath. No regrets, okay?”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433241ra/871726.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“When I met you...somehow you healed me. From the inside out, the outside in. We conquered fears together, we learned, we laughed, and we loved. I swear, you caused my heart to soar more in the past few months than it has in my entire existence. My heart is whole because you chose to share yours with me...”<br><br>--Wes<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I <b>cried</b>, <b>laughed</b>, <b>mothereffing swooned</b>, <b>learned</b> about life, and fell <b>in love</b>. This book did this to me. It is one of my <b>favorites</b> for sure, because what an <b>experience</b>. I was <b>never</b> annoyed with the heroine, and I <b>adored</b> the hero. The ending was really <b>wonderful</b>. I mean I <b>knew</b> it was going to happen, but was still so <b>happy</b> when I read it. There were <b>so</b> many nuggets of wisdom that it really made you <b>think</b>. We always <b>forget</b> to <b>appreciate</b> the little things. I also enjoyed that little <b>surprise</b> we got. I was tearing up with <b>happiness</b>. So don't worry people, there is an <b>HEA</b>. Seriously, you must <b>go</b> and read this book <b>NOW!</b> I am not kidding. <b>SO GOOD!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433241ra/871727.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Sometimes when we think God has written The End, what he really means is The Beginning.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16208306578429498623"> <b>4 Real Sweet Bucket-list Stars!</b><br/><br/><i> <b>”Maybe it’s not in the perfection of life that things make sense, but in the chaos.”</b></i><br/><br/>This is the story of Kiersten and Wes. <br/>Kiersten is mourning the loss of her parents, she never had the chance of saying goodbye to them and she closed herself to the world, afraid of having to feel loss again. She is kind of a broken soul. <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434841ra/878087.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Enter Wes.   <span id="freeText16208306578429498623" style="display:none"> <b>4 Real Sweet Bucket-list Stars!</b><br><br><i> <b>”Maybe it’s not in the perfection of life that things make sense, but in the chaos.”</b></i><br><br>This is the story of Kiersten and Wes. <br>Kiersten is mourning the loss of her parents, she never had the chance of saying goodbye to them and she closed herself to the world, afraid of having to feel loss again. She is kind of a broken soul. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434841ra/878087.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Enter Wes. Tv show star, completely hot and unfortunately, extremely sick.<br>So he knows he can’t fall in love with her, not when he doesn’t know how much more time he could have and especially when she doesn’t know about his condition and when she won’t be able to deal with the loss of more people in her life. <br>But the thing is: neither of them can’t help it. <br>When it’s real there’s nothing you can do to stop it. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434841ra/878088.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was a real sweet reading. Both Kiersten and Wes are amazing characters and I felt connected to them since page one. The supportive characters were also pretty good and I’m hoping we’ll be able to read Gabe’s story. <br>There were really heartbreaking moments but the story is so beautiful that you can almost ignore the angst behind it. <br>The only reason I’m not giving it five stars it’s because it was a bit too sickly sweet, and had too much motivational talk. I mean, there has to be a limit of “in how many different ways can you say to enjoy life”. <br>Other than that, a pretty great book.<br>You should try it ;) </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer707676785" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3689868922653766766">I LIKED it, didn’t absolutely love it, and I see that I am in the minority from most of my friends. It was a nice story, he was nice, she was nice, the friends were very nice. Dad was nice, Uncle was nice…. Have I turned into someone who NEEDs a bit of angst in a book. I don’t think so. Maybe I really need the characters to be older. I am 47, so reading about 18 year olds might just be a bit too much for me. Overall a nice story, Will I check out other books by this author – probably – have read</span>
  <span id="freeText3689868922653766766" style="display:none">I LIKED it, didn’t absolutely love it, and I see that I am in the minority from most of my friends. It was a nice story, he was nice, she was nice, the friends were very nice. Dad was nice, Uncle was nice…. Have I turned into someone who NEEDs a bit of angst in a book. I don’t think so. Maybe I really need the characters to be older. I am 47, so reading about 18 year olds might just be a bit too much for me. Overall a nice story, Will I check out other books by this author – probably – have read one of her other books and I did enjoy it so, Yes, I probably will.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434907i/878252._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380946855i/3464432._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I suppose, eventhough this book did have a “darker” theme going through it, it wasl still …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380946855i/3464433.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3689868922653766766" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_699685483" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/699685483" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/699685483?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to • Lisa • by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=my-friend-anna-and-her-weepy-reads">my-friend-anna-and-her-weepy-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer699685483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5415991502631712110"><b>FOUR WOLF STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I'd never felt so alive as when that girl, that perfectly strange girl who I'd only met days before, was near me."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394477972i/8857945._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You know those type of books that you feel like everyone has read but you? Well, this book was exactly one of those and I can't tell you any other reason for the delay in starting this book other than I didn't think I would be ready for what I knew would be a tear jerker and I can report with satisfaction that this book definitely needs to be read with a good sup</span>
  <span id="freeText5415991502631712110" style="display:none"><b>FOUR WOLF STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I'd never felt so alive as when that girl, that perfectly strange girl who I'd only met days before, was near me."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394477972i/8857945._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know those type of books that you feel like everyone has read but you? Well, this book was exactly one of those and I can't tell you any other reason for the delay in starting this book other than I didn't think I would be ready for what I knew would be a tear jerker and I can report with satisfaction that this book definitely needs to be read with a good supply of tissues at hand and a large glass of your preferred alcohol beverage. Wonderfully written to young adult perfection this book delivered a well rounded story about love, life and finding 'the one'. Here are my 'I've finally read this book' thoughts ...<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>After facing personal tragedy in her life, Kiersten Rowe never believed she would have the strength or faith to move forward to a place of self forgiveness and peace. But after finding the perfect friendship in the most unexpected place, Kiersten may just have to start realising that she may just have found the road to true happiness. Weston Micheals appears to have it all, he's the star quarter back, loved by all and to top it off he's the son of a famous actor so why does he feel like his life is on borrowed time? When Kiersten and Weston's lives collide it starts the beginning of a special friendship that neither of them could have ever imagined, their lives will never be the same.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394477972i/8857946._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>Rachel Van Dyken in my opinion is an author who is able to write successful love-themed stories within a different range of genres. From contemporary story telling, to romantic comedies and suspense she obviously can offer her talent across the board and after reading this story I am able confirm that I am sold on her ability to write a perfectly well told 'young/new adult' novel. The characters were the selling point of 'Ruin', both the hero and heroine were notably likeable and I can confirm that predictably I have officially joined the many fans of Weston Micheals. Van Dyken must have a super extraordinary imagination when it comes to creating heroes or she is extremely lucky and has gorgeously swoony men in her life that she is able to model her characters on, Weston is a character that screams love-me-forever-readers, he won't be a character that is forgotten any time soon. I especially enjoy a story that also includes fall-in-love worthy secondary characters and I can already confess that I'm excited to read about Gabe in the next book of the series. This story has a wonderful theme of healing, friendship and heart break it was all delivered with a depth and sweetness that prevented if from being too depressing. There isn't too much steam in the story telling but any novel that can keep my heart racing without the added schmexy love-making wins points for me. Overall I'd describe 'Ruin' as a delightful coming of age story of faith, love and the hope that finding that one who changes your life is enough to make a difference that counts. I feel like I've read a heartwarming novel that is as lovely as it it heart breaking and I can't say that I have any regrets. once again this author has given me a romantic fix that I so crave, so to you Rachel Van Dyken, thank you.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394477972i/8857947._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>As much as I enjoyed this novel overall, the beginning had a slow start for my reading tastes. I did feel like I was thrown into a instant love connection that I felt came out of nowhere. That in itself normally distracts from a higher rating but for such a short novel I found my myself surprised by the last 40% of the story-telling and I was won over by the emotions that I felt as the story of Wes and Kiersten was concluded. Rachel van Dyken has definitely grabbed my attention with this series and I'm happily going to carry on to see what transpires with other characters that I've been introduced to.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394477973i/8857948._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>I laughed, I cried, I had those unmistakable 'my-heart-feels-like-it-could-burst-moments' that makes a book worth reading, so as you can see this book won my heart over and I'm more than glad that I finally took the plunge to read a book that has been on my reading radar for some time now. Would I recommend to fellow romance addicts? Yes go and fall in love but one word of caution don't start this book without wine, tissues and your next light hearted 'to be read' book to start straight after. If like me, you are late to the party don't delay, go grab it readers. Enjoy, kisses.<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5415991502631712110" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2800980048" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2800980048" />
    <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com"><img alt="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570843185p2/70316517.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2800980048?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️" href="/user/show/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com">Ꮗ€♫◗☿ ❤️ ilikebooksbest.com ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/40521873-ruin">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/70316517-ilikebooksbest-com?shelf=tear-jerkers">tear-jerkers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2800980048" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer810246786459534341"><b>Terrific book with all the feels.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574255781i/28480856.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574259059i/28481129.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Very enjoyable yet emotional book. I really liked this book overall, though in a way it gave me the same feeling I had the first time I watched the movie Titanic. I knew going in that the ship was going to hit that iceberg and the majority of its passengers would die, but I was still hoping for a different outcome and even though the ship sank, the story was so good. This story begins with a prologue that is written in a way that it is hard to tell exactly what i</span>
  <span id="freeText810246786459534341" style="display:none"><b>Terrific book with all the feels.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574255781i/28480856.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1574259059i/28481129.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Very enjoyable yet emotional book. I really liked this book overall, though in a way it gave me the same feeling I had the first time I watched the movie Titanic. I knew going in that the ship was going to hit that iceberg and the majority of its passengers would die, but I was still hoping for a different outcome and even though the ship sank, the story was so good. This story begins with a prologue that is written in a way that it is hard to tell exactly what is happening, but you know it is bad. Then the first chapter begins three months prior to what happened in the prologue.<br><br>The story takes place at the University of Washington, where new freshman student Kiersten has a nightmare and her roommate Lisa runs in from her own bedroom after hearing Kiersten screaming. Kiersten blows it off as night terrors, but Lisa is a great roommate and sleeps the rest of the night on the floor. Of course we, as readers know that when a girl in a romance novel has nightmares it usually stems from some type of past trauma. Though we are kept in the dark as to what exactly. <br><br>The following day at some point, Kiersten’s inner monologue tells us that she takes medication, for either depression or anxiety, though we don’t find out much more than that. Kiersten meets a guy with blonde hair and an eight pack when she literally runs into him. She apparently comes from a very small town and gets embarrassed easily. She ends up running into him again and though she wants to stay away, he seems interested in her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1574259059ra/28481128.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Her roommate Lisa and Lisa’s cousin Gabe fill Kiersten in on who he is afterwards. The guy is Weston Michaels, the current Big Man on Campus, son of one of the wealthiest men in the world, and quarterback of the University football team. He told Kiersten that he doesn’t date Freshmen, but he wants to be friends. <br><br>The romance between the two main characters starts out very sweet, but there are all kinds of things going on. Weston has a secret and has things in his past that are alluded to, part of which the reader can guess at due to the hints and what he says and thinks. However, I was trying to guess at so much through the greater part of the book. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1574255781ra/28480859.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was also wondering for quite a while what happened to Kiersten that left her medicated and with nightmares. In addition to all the secrets, the relationship is strange, they both seem to not want a relationship but they also seem to want to be together. Weston is always thinking and saying how attracted he is to her, but he just wants to be friends.<br><br>Kiersten is a bit dense in some ways though she is a likable heroine. She thinks Wes couldn’t possibly like her because he is a senior and she is a freshman and he garners attention wherever he goes but she is from a very small town and is a Virgin. It bothered me a tiny bit because her roommate mentions how beautiful she is, and he is always saying things like how much he wants her. Maybe because he used to be a player, she thinks his wanting her is different than his wanting to date her. <br><br>This book is written in a way that you end up really liking all the characters. Lisa’ cousin Gabe becomes Kiersten’s best friend and a bit of a protector. The relationship between them is cool. Almost like a big brother. Weston has an “entourage” as he and everyone at the University calls them. They are the bodyguards his father hired. Weston’s father turns out to be much less stern than you would think for someone in his position and Kiersten’s Uncle Jobob (Yes Joe-bob) is a nice guy. All of the characters are well developed and have clear voices of their own.<br><br>The writing is very good. Like I said earlier, there are secrets that the reader knows partially but I was kept guessing on a lot of things so I truly couldn’t put the book down until I finished. The world-building in the book is really on point. I could totally picture the campus, the dorms, Weston’s father’s home, and all the places they went. The romance was great. Weston and Kiersten developed true love over the course of the book. It was not a hot and steamy book, though their kisses were off the charts. And I really enjoyed it. The book is a standalone and I bought the next two books if that tells you anything.<br><br><u>
  <b>Buddy Read with Anonymous Girl</b>

    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/653633062?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer653633062" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6399682084967951550">5--I'm officially <b>RUIN</b>ed--Stars!!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"You rescued me and I found my ruin. I'm ruined for you--and I won't ever be the same. It's the greatest gift anyone's ever given me."</i>
</b><br/><br/>First of all....big fan of Rachel Van Dyken. The cover on this book--SMOKING HOT! Really had no idea what to expect--definitely wasn't expecting what I got....in the BEST. WAY. POSSIBLE.<br/><br/>Expect to do a lot of this....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/619725.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And a shit ton of this....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/455016.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was a fantastic read. Sucked me in from the first page. I immediatly fell in love</span>
  <span id="freeText6399682084967951550" style="display:none">5--I'm officially <b>RUIN</b>ed--Stars!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"You rescued me and I found my ruin. I'm ruined for you--and I won't ever be the same. It's the greatest gift anyone's ever given me."</i>
</b><br><br>First of all....big fan of Rachel Van Dyken. The cover on this book--SMOKING HOT! Really had no idea what to expect--definitely wasn't expecting what I got....in the BEST. WAY. POSSIBLE.<br><br>Expect to do a lot of this....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/619725.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And a shit ton of this....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/455016.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was a fantastic read. Sucked me in from the first page. I immediatly fell in love with Weston Michel! And I loved Kiersten too. This was a real tear jerker people....so grab those Kleenex! <br><br><b>
  <i>"Favorite everything. You're my favorite. Out of all the things I could have in the world that would be my favorite, you win. You win all of it."</i>
</b><br><br>Kiersten is a freshman in college. She lost her parents in a tragic diving accident and suffers from depression and anxiety as a result. Her first day of school she meets Weston Michel. Weston is a senior, the RA in her dorm and is the campus stud. He also lost his mom and brother. <br><br>Watching Weston and Kiersten fall in love was just beautiful--lame I know, but it was. Their banter amongst each other was so fun and I can't even begin to tell you what this book did to my heart--good and bad. Really just a really touching story. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Then that's what I am," Wes whispered, "I'm thankful for you. I thank God for you. Maybe He can see me after all. In this moment I can believe he cares."<br><br>"Don't give up yet. Sometimes when we think God has written The End, what he really means is The Beginning."</i>
</b><br><br>I know I'm giving you next to nothing when it comes to the story but you really just have to experience it yourself--it's worth it!!! I can't recommend this book enough. <br><br>This was one of my favorite quotes--honestly, I highlighted almost the entire book. It was <b>THAT</b> great!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>"Every time you close your eyes, regardless of where I am or where you are, I want you to remember this. Wherever I am, whatever I'm doing, alive or dead, young or old, my heart will always be with yours. Every beat you feel against your fingertips..." His finger tapped against my chest, once, twice."...is me calling out to you. It's you returning the call. It's us talking, communicating, bonding, sharing. Living--Kiersten, it's us living. There may come a time in your life when your heart will have to beat for mine...but you'll have to carry on if I can't. Just like there may come a time when I have to do the same for you. But in the end, one of us will always carry on this." He tapped again. "So there's never a reason to be afraid of running out of time--because we keep our own time."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/632033.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Weston:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423155ra/842887.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6399682084967951550" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

When the guy you fall in love with kisses you- it better put this kiss to shame- if it doesn't then he isn't the right guy. Because I'm going to do a damn good job, and I want that guy that earns you, that takes that heart of yours and holds it in the palm of his hands....I wa</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText15897532730350532525" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434150i/874153._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>This guy.....Wes.....he invaded my heart!</b> I wanted to sacrifice my heart for his !!!❤❤❤ I loved him !!!<br><br><blockquote>"I'm going to make it so hard for you to forget this first kiss that you don't want anyone else kissing you ever again. When the guy you fall in love with kisses you- it better put this kiss to shame- if it doesn't then he isn't the right guy. Because I'm going to do a damn good job, and I want that guy that earns you, that takes that heart of yours and holds it in the palm of his hands....I want that guy to be able to make you feel things I'll just be tapping into. do you understand, Kiersten? I want the Earth to shift"</blockquote><br><br>First off I want to say...<br><b>DAMN.THAT.PROLOGUE.</b><br><br><blockquote>I'd lost the love of my life- my best friend. We hadn't been given enough time- and I hated God for taking everyone from me. I hated that in the end, I would always be alone to mourn the loss of those I loved.</blockquote><br><br>yeah...that prologue....So luckily I was ready for this. I am on a personal quest of stay-with-me-forever type of books. This one delivered and then some. I totally expected to cry my heart out but in the interim....I fell in love as they fell in love. I laughed when they laughed. I lost count of the times Wes had me swooning with his ridiculously romantic gestures! <br><br><b>Weakness is just pain leaving the body.<br><br>My new job description is making you laugh and chasing away the bad dreams.<br><br>You think of their death as torture. I think of it as peace. I see them holding hands into the darkness, and I see them smiling.<br><br>For the first time in a year, I wanted to live- because I wanted tot spend every freaking day watching her open her eyes to the world. </b><br><br>I can't say too much more without giving away the whole story. This story was a lot about Faith. It was heartfelt and emotional and truly amazing.<br><br><br><blockquote>"I can tell you have a good heart because the minute I met you, I wanted to fight for it."<br>"That's how you can tell when someone has a good heart? When you want to start a war?<br>"Nah. When you want to be the one to make it beat."</blockquote><br><br><b>wherever I am, whatever I am doing, alive or dead, young or old, my heart will always be with yours.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434150i/874154.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434150i/874155._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>10. Fall in love<br>11. Get heart broken<br>12. Fall in love anyway<br><br><br>So in closing I wanted to say...this book really surprised me. I have been around the block and if any of you know me, my preference is weepy-steamy reads...this book has that special place in my book heart for my PG13 squeaky-clean reads ranking up there with <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10194514.Pushing_the_Limits__Pushing_the_Limits___1_" title="Pushing the Limits (Pushing the Limits, #1) by Katie McGarry" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1322770025s/10194514.jpg" alt="Pushing the Limits (Pushing the Limits, #1) by Katie McGarry" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13122965.Callum___Harper__Sleepless___1_" title="Callum &amp; Harper (Sleepless, #1) by Fisher Amelie" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1322521960s/13122965.jpg" alt="Callum &amp; Harper (Sleepless, #1) by Fisher Amelie" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13366929.What_I_Didn_t_Say" title="What I Didn't Say by Keary Taylor" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1355090370s/13366929.jpg" alt="What I Didn't Say by Keary Taylor" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13372690.Slammed__Slammed___1_" title="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1328530463s/13372690.jpg" alt="Slammed (Slammed, #1) by Colleen Hoover" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> ...that made me, this self-professed puta, have a full body blush and falling in young love all over again. Just beautiful!!!!<br><br><b>Even though I was waiting and waiting and waiting for Wolf to pounce Lamb ;) </b> just sayin!!!!</span>
