<div id="review_1031413360" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1031413360" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1031413360?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1031413360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15242775790918393127"><i>
  <b>“You rescued me and I found my ruin. I’m ruined for you– and I won’t ever be the same.”</b>
</i> <br/><br/>This was just an okay book. It wasn’t that great, but it wasn’t crazy bad either. What I love about this book was <b>Weston</b>. He’s one of the best male leads I’ve encountered in a New Adult book. He actually reminds me of <b>Cam</b> from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_' title='Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wait for You</a>. Anyways, I really love characters with a great sense of humor. <b>Kiersten</b> was also a great character. She wasn’t exactly the most likable of people to read about at firs</span>
  <span id="freeText15242775790918393127" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“You rescued me and I found my ruin. I’m ruined for you– and I won’t ever be the same.”</b>
</i> <br /><br />This was just an okay book. It wasn’t that great, but it wasn’t crazy bad either. What I love about this book was <b>Weston</b>. He’s one of the best male leads I’ve encountered in a New Adult book. He actually reminds me of <b>Cam</b> from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Wait for You</a>. Anyways, I really love characters with a great sense of humor. <b>Kiersten</b> was also a great character. She wasn’t exactly the most likable of people to read about at first, but I was glad that I quickly warmed up to her. I love her enthusiasm to step away from her nightmares and grief over her parent’s death.<br /><br />The book mainly focuses on <b>illness, grief, hope,</b> and <b>love</b>. It was not 100% emotionally-packed because there was humor in it which made the book a light read, so don’t expect it to really tear your hearts like what some illnesses and death books do. The main concerns I have with this book were 1.) the <b>insta-love</b>, 2.) the <b>un-original concept</b>, and 3.) <b>some clichés</b>. The romance was good and it was sweet, but majority of it didn’t grab me at all.<br /><br />Otherwise, the story was still a nice piece of fiction. It has life lessons to teach you and it also inspires you to never give up and continue to fight no matter how hard life takes you at some point.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Sometimes when we think God has written The End, what He really means is The Beginning.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Rating: 3 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="15242775790918393127" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692881121" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9831909384047598700">4 ★'s <br/><br/><i>"You rescued me and I found my ruin."</i><br/><br/>Weston and Kiersten meet on her first day of college in a quite intriguing way. They both are drawn to each other but they also see something in each other that inspires them to not give up. <br/><br/>Right away, we know something's going on with Weston. It takes a bit to get the full story and it's not pretty. The blurb gives us hints of what's to come but it's hard to prepare. <br/><br/>Kiersten has her own problems and she's just starting to come up for air. College is </span>
  <span id="freeText9831909384047598700" style="display:none">4 ★'s <br><br><i>"You rescued me and I found my ruin."</i><br><br>Weston and Kiersten meet on her first day of college in a quite intriguing way. They both are drawn to each other but they also see something in each other that inspires them to not give up. <br><br>Right away, we know something's going on with Weston. It takes a bit to get the full story and it's not pretty. The blurb gives us hints of what's to come but it's hard to prepare. <br><br>Kiersten has her own problems and she's just starting to come up for air. College is a big step for her but fortunately she has Wes and he's more than she thought she would ever need. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466180805ra/19450196.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wes' life has also been hard...it's really quite depressing but the romance between these two gives you hope and makes the book hard to put down. <br><br>There is a religious element that caught me by surprise. This is my first book by Rachel Van Dyken so I'm not sure if this is a common theme of hers. I had conflicting feelings about some it...liking some parts while others were pretty out there. <br><br>Overall, these two have a great romance and that's what I enjoyed even if it was a bit quick. I'm definitely looking forward to reading their novella, <i>Fearless</i> to find out what else happened with these two. <br><br>There's also a book for each of their friends, Gabe and Lisa, and they both sound very intriguing...especially Gabe! ;)</span>

<div id="review_692933266" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692933266" />
    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692933266?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692933266" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16580300635754480954"><br/><br/>4 ruined stars!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Don’t give up yet. Sometimes when we think God has written The End , what he really means is The Beginning .”</i>
</b><br/><br/>So.. Its taken me a few days to write this review because I've been gathering my feelings about it.<br/><br/>I have to start off by saying that this book was excellently written.<br/><br/>With different POV's we get the emotions of two totally different characters which in my book are brought together by sheer fate.<br/><br/>Kiersten is such an innocent girl which grief and depression has taken ove</span>
  <span id="freeText16580300635754480954" style="display:none"><br><br>4 ruined stars!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Don’t give up yet. Sometimes when we think God has written The End , what he really means is The Beginning .”</i>
</b><br><br>So.. Its taken me a few days to write this review because I've been gathering my feelings about it.<br><br>I have to start off by saying that this book was excellently written.<br><br>With different POV's we get the emotions of two totally different characters which in my book are brought together by sheer fate.<br><br>Kiersten is such an innocent girl which grief and depression has taken over leaving her an empty soul.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432793i/870498.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wes Michels... The boy who everything thinks has it all... Money, fame, looks.. Little do these people know that Wes wants something that no one can provide... Time...<br><br><b>
  <i>"It was the first real hug I’d received since my brother had died. I didn’t tell her that, but in that moment, hugging her, comforting her… Death didn’t look as bad anymore. The future didn’t look as bleak. Because when she pulled back… when her eyes met mine, I saw hope."</i>
</b><br><br>Wes and Kiersten become friends and conquer lists of "To Do's" in life but litter do they know that these things are for completely differently reasons.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Because you never knew when a moment would be your last. So why not soak up every last memory?"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432793i/870499.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For Kiersten its to bring the light back into her life and for Wes... It was so bring that something into her life before time wasn't on his side anymore.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432793i/870500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"It’s human nature to assume that we have that sort of control over what happens to us, but the truth is… life happens and sometimes you’re too late. Hell, sometimes you’re too early. Sometimes you make the wrong choice just like sometimes you make the right one. The only time people ever use those three is when things don’t go the right way. People don’t question themselves when things are going well. They question themselves when things have gone to hell.”</i>
</b><br><br>Offcourse Wes didn't allow himself or Kiersten to fall in love because of the situation but these things are unplanned.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432793i/870501.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When we find out the real reasons and how bad it really is, there are really heart breaking moments.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Wherever I am, whatever I’m doing, alive or dead, young or old, my heart will always be with yours. Every beat you feel against your fingertips…” His finger tapped against my chest, once, twice. “…is me calling out to you. It’s you returning the call. It’s us talking, communicating, bonding, sharing. Living — Kiersten, it’s us living. There may come a time in your life when your heart will have to beat for mine… but you’ll have to carry on if I can’t. Just like there may come a time when I have to do the same for you. But in the end, one of us will always carry on this.” He tapped again. “So there’s never a reason to be afraid of running out of time — because we keep our own.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432793i/870502._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"She has absolutely no idea what she does to me… She’s my medicine, my cure, my everything. If only hearts could heal that way — through someone else’s beating."</b><br><br>Wes Micheals has Ruined me too...<br><br><b>
  <i>"I can tell you have a good heart…” I sighed, opening the door to the outside. “…because the minute I met you, I wanted to fight for it.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432793i/870503.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Miracles in life do happen if we... <br><i>Believe</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432793i/870504.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You rescued me and I found my ruin.” I bit down on my lip. “I’m ruined for you — and I won’t ever be the same. It’s the greatest gift anyone’s ever given me.”</i>
</b><br><br>All the characters in this book are really awesome so if you looking for a funny, emotional, heartbreaking and heartwarming read, this is definitely worth a read! <br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer684271363" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8222507542368421147">Ruin wasn't what I expected, it was better! It is a story that I didn't foresee, a topic I didn't think could be tackled, and a journey I didn't want to end. Ruin is raw; pure raw emotion. You will cry, your breathing will hitch, you will tell yourself 'this can't be happening' over and over again -- and you will continue to read because this story is powerful and has the ability to change you -- change your outlook on life, on love, on time. I feel blessed to have read this book (yes I just sai</span>
  <span id="freeText8222507542368421147" style="display:none">Ruin wasn't what I expected, it was better! It is a story that I didn't foresee, a topic I didn't think could be tackled, and a journey I didn't want to end. Ruin is raw; pure raw emotion. You will cry, your breathing will hitch, you will tell yourself 'this can't be happening' over and over again -- and you will continue to read because this story is powerful and has the ability to change you -- change your outlook on life, on love, on time. I feel blessed to have read this book (yes I just said 'blessed' in a book review). Ultimately Wes and Kiersten's story will become a movie in your mind as you experience it first-hand. Gabe and Lisa will become your friends too because this story feels real. Wes, Kiersten, Gabe and Lisa show what true friendship and love is all about. Because you never know what hand life will deal you, only you can decide what to do with the hand you are dealt. Ruin is heart-wrenching, packs an emotional punch (or two) and takes you on a journey you never thought you would take. Words honestly cannot describe how incredible this novel is. Ruin spans multiple genres because this inspiring novel will bring even the harshest critic to tears.<br /> "Do it afraid." ~Wes<br />"...we'll keep our own time." ~Kiersten<br />I received a copy of this book for free. This is my honest review.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1736500015?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13710123-barbara?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13710123-barbara?shelf=perfect-hero">perfect-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1736500015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7447781558901615486">This book...it slayed me. Logically, I knew there would be a happy ending. I mean, many of my GR friends read it and 5 starred it. But my heart just kept hurting. <br/><br/>Poor Kiersten...after tragically losing her parents in a diving accident she's depressed...just barely living. She literally walks right into Wes, the senior, rich football player. Then, a beautiful friendship forms that turns into more. They both help each other. Wes helps her to start living again and Kiersten makes him want to fight</span>
  <span id="freeText7447781558901615486" style="display:none">This book...it slayed me. Logically, I knew there would be a happy ending. I mean, many of my GR friends read it and 5 starred it. But my heart just kept hurting. <br /><br />Poor Kiersten...after tragically losing her parents in a diving accident she's depressed...just barely living. She literally walks right into Wes, the senior, rich football player. Then, a beautiful friendship forms that turns into more. They both help each other. Wes helps her to start living again and Kiersten makes him want to fight...to live. <br /><br />Wes was absolutely perfect. The things he does for Kiersten, helping her through her list and his words, were just...well perfect. <br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>His lips moved to my cheek. “And know that in this moment… you’re not living in the woulda, shoulda, coulda zone. You’re exactly where the universe wants you to be.” “In your bed?” I grinned. “Nah.” His mouth met mine. “In my arms.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m going to devour you with my eyes. I’m going to look at every inch of skin, memorize it, store it in the little box in my head labeled the most beautiful girl in the world. I’m going to hold you until you’re ready for me to let go, and then, when you float on your own, I’m going to keep staring, keep wanting, keep desiring, until I have to go jump into the Sound.”~Wes</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />I found it amazing how Kiersten actually began to live. Wes was so good to her and helped to pull her out of the hole she had buried herself in. She then found strength to help Wes and pull him up. <br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m ruined for you —and I won’t ever be the same. It’s the greatest gift anyone’s ever given me.”~Kiersten </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />Not to mention Gabe. He was a wonderful friend to them both. He needs his happy ending too.<br /><br />So feelings and all, this book was amazing. I laughed and I cried...it slayed me. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_693049608" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/693049608" />
    <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b"><img alt="M. ~ B&amp;B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435261660p2/14479657.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/693049608?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M. ~ B&amp;B" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b">M. ~ B&amp;B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer693049608" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1546283682723150142">For once, I don't have much to say about a book. I hoped to love this, but unfortunately I didn't. The story is about two characters who have both experienced loss and grief. The hero in this story is sick, but he doesn't tell anyone about it. When he meets the heroine, he decides to help her and show her how to live life. In the process, he gets his love for life and living back too. <br/><br/>One of my biggest problems here was that I didn't connect with the characters at all. It all seemed very rushed </span>
  <span id="freeText1546283682723150142" style="display:none">For once, I don't have much to say about a book. I hoped to love this, but unfortunately I didn't. The story is about two characters who have both experienced loss and grief. The hero in this story is sick, but he doesn't tell anyone about it. When he meets the heroine, he decides to help her and show her how to live life. In the process, he gets his love for life and living back too. <br /><br />One of my biggest problems here was that I didn't connect with the characters at all. It all seemed very rushed to me. There was hardly any build-up to their relationship either. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They were friends, then we got a fast forward of two months and suddenly they decided to be boyfriend/girlfriend. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />The story felt very unoriginal. It felt like I had read all of it before. I'm fine with stories not being completely original, but at least make sure the execution is amazing. I thought it was all pretty cliche and kinda superficial even though the message is supposed to be very deep. The writing was okay, but it didn't grab me at all. <br /><br />The banter between the characters was cute and funny, but I didn't feel like I knew the characters. It was all just so random. If the book hadn't been so short, I would've taken the DNF route. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1546283682723150142" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I just remember Ruin to be very endearing, heart wrenching and good!<br/><br/>A lot of people told me to read Ruin and said to read it with tissues and I didn’t pick it up for the longest time because of that.   <span id="freeText11783718726757617679" style="display:none"><b>5 CRY MY BLOODY EYES OUT Stars</b><br><br>Again, I read Ruin, during the holidays and did not write a review right away. Wes can’t get into a relationship with Kiresten, but the chemistry and attraction is there! It’s a sweet story with a very dark undertone. You feel all the emotions and it kind of makes you wonder what you are doing with your life.<br><br>Despite the heart ache, the sadness, there’s just a lot of awe, melt-your-heart moments that keep you glued to the pages. <br><br>You must read RUIN!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18134249.Ruin__Ruin___1_" title="Ruin (Ruin, #1) by Rachel Van Dyken" rel="nofollow noopener">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3898049-heather?shelf=friends-2-lovers">friends-2-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3898049-heather?shelf=author-i-love">author-i-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer696422041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12245353779817549599"><p><strong>This book ruined me for all other books.</strong> I normally like the more adult books with hot and steamy romance in them. This was an adult book but it was all about the romance and the emotional and mental relationship and not about the physical aspects. This book was <strong>perfection</strong>. It has earned a coveted spot on my <strong>all time favorites</strong> list.</p><br/><img alt='' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433283i/871833.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><p>Kiersten is a college freshman. She has been through a lot in the last few years and it was a stretch to get her to go off on her own. She has to prove to herself tha</p></span>
  <span id="freeText12245353779817549599" style="display:none"><p><strong>This book ruined me for all other books.</strong> I normally like the more adult books with hot and steamy romance in them. This was an adult book but it was all about the romance and the emotional and mental relationship and not about the physical aspects. This book was <strong>perfection</strong>. It has earned a coveted spot on my <strong>all time favorites</strong> list.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433283i/871833.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>Kiersten is a college freshman. She has been through a lot in the last few years and it was a stretch to get her to go off on her own. She has to prove to herself that she can be happy again. She has to prove to everyone around her that she is going to make it. She has spent the last several years holed up in her room living in a sort of haze. Kiersten has a lot to be afraid of and her fears are controlling her life.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433283i/871834.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>Weston is the college quarterback. He is a senior and he is also out to prove something. He is out to prove to the world that he is strong. He has to be strong enough. He has to push through and the only way he can do that is by helping save a lost college freshman. He can's change the past, he can't change his future, but he is going to help make someones life brighter.<br><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433283i/871835._SX540_.jpg" width="373" height="248" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></p><br><p>Wes sets out to be Kiersten's life coach. He sees her darkness and her fears and he decides to make it his goal to help her conquer them. They create a list. A list of fears that Kiersten will overcome. We immediately feels drawn to Kiersten but he places her firmly in the "just friends" category. He takes away her nightmares and she makes his heart beat stronger.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871836.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>There is no denying the attraction and Wes decides to take the leap of faith. He is going to let Kiersten in. He plans to tell her everything. He only hopes that his own fears don't drag her down with him. He is living his life at full throttle. Together they set out to be stronger and to be better.</p><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871837.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><em>“I’m going to make it so hard for you to forget this first kiss that you don’t want anyone else kissing you ever again. When the guy you fall in love with kisses you — it better put this kiss to shame — if it doesn’t, then he isn’t the right guy. Because I’m going to do a damn good job, and I want the guy that earns you, that takes that heart of yours and holds it in the palm of his hands… I want that guy to be able to make you feel things I’ll just be tapping into. Do you understand, Kiersten?” </em><br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871838.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Time is not on their side. As Kiersten comes to understand what is truly happening with Wes, she has to make a choice. She can let it scare her away, or she can stand tall and fight.<br><br><em>“So there’s never a reason to be afraid of running out of time — because we keep our own.” </em><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871839.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><em>“Wherever I am, whatever I'm doing, alive or dead, young or old, my heart will always be with yours. Every beat you feel against your fingertips..." His fingers tapped against my chest, once, twice. "... is me calling out to you. It's you returning the call. It's us talking, communicating, bonding, sharing, Living -- Kiersten, it's us living.” </em><br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871840.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>Wes has finally found his reason to live, and it may be too late for them. He has to have faith and be strong and hope against all hope that he gets his happily ever after.</p><br><p>
  <em>“You may not see every single piece of the puzzle that creates your life -- you may not see every move the grand chess player makes -- but know, He is in complete control of the game board. Sometimes certain pieces are moved or knocked over to make room for new ones. Other times, things happen because of the world we live in. But everything in the end, will always turn out for good. It's a nice promise, isn't it? To know there's a reason for it all?” </em>
  <br>
  <img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871841.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><p>This was me....</p><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871842.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><p>Me, ugly crying with my Kindle. <strong>This book crushed me!</strong> And it gave me hope. It is the most amazing story. I literally had goosebumps. It was that good.</p><br><p>
  <strong>Well done Rachel Van Dyken!</strong>
  <br>
  <img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433283ra/871843.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><p>I have liked everything I have read from this author but this one really takes the cake. This book was told from both points of view. This is a quintessential new adult genre book. Both characters are coming into their own as young adults and exploring more adult issues. Wes and his family have been through so much it just broke my heart. He was so sweet and adorable with Kiersten. He was a little obsessed with her long red hair. She was a little in love with his eight pack abs. She has had to deal with more in her short life than anyone should. Through it all, together, they find love in the most unexpected place.</p><br><p>I was so afraid to read the end....so afraid. I did not want the sad ending that I was afraid of. Without giving spoilers there is a happily ever after. It was amazing. <strong>I love, love, loved it</strong>. If I could give more than five stars...I would.</p><br><p>
  <a href="http://johnstohbibliomaniac.files.wordpress.com/2013/05/red_star_5_of_5-bb0a37528bbb2ff1f4b732afff2bb9681.png" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img alt="red_star_5_of_5-bb0a37528bbb2ff1f4b732afff2bb968" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378039i/733461.png" width="75" height="15" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="12245353779817549599" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_683876209" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/683876209" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/683876209?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=cried-big-fat-ugly-tears">cried-big-fat-ugly-tears</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer683876209" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1751659222676610843">I can't remember when a book has had me swooning and crying in equal measure!!<br/>"Ruin" is a beautifully written story of a once in a lifetime love that has the power to make miracles possible.<br/>I absolutely positively freaking loved this book and practically highlighted it entirely!!<br/>There were so many beautiful excerpts throughout.<br/><br/>Kiersten Rowe is starting her freshman year at the University of Washington.<br/>She's trying to break out of the shell that her depression and anxiety have encased her in, whe</span>
  <span id="freeText1751659222676610843" style="display:none">I can't remember when a book has had me swooning and crying in equal measure!!<br>"Ruin" is a beautifully written story of a once in a lifetime love that has the power to make miracles possible.<br>I absolutely positively freaking loved this book and practically highlighted it entirely!!<br>There were so many beautiful excerpts throughout.<br><br>Kiersten Rowe is starting her freshman year at the University of Washington.<br>She's trying to break out of the shell that her depression and anxiety have encased her in, when her parents died several years ago.<br>She's from a small town and has never had any experience with boys.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps63e06583.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431504i/865933._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps63e06583.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then she literally crashes into Wes and his "8 pack abs" on freshman orientation day.<br>Wes Michels is beyond perfection and sure to be a book boyfriend contender.<br>He's drop dead gorgeous, football quarterback, and dear god he says the most amazingly beautiful things I've ever read.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps83067453.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431504i/865934._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps83067453.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>"Every time you close your eyes, regardless of where I am or where you are, I want you to remember this." His fingers laced with mine and then he pressed my hand against my own chest. "Wherever I am, whatever I'm doing, alive or dead, young or old, my heart will always be with yours. Every beat you feel against your fingertips..."</b>
</i><br><br>Wes charms his way into Kiersten's life and he becomes her savior.<br>Her dragonslayer :)<br>He helps her realize it's ok to have fear...to do things afraid!!<br>He gives her the greatest gift of all...true love.<br><br><i>
  <b>Wes had single-handedly put me at ease, as well as wisely taught me one thing. Control what you can, love what you can, and the rest, well...the rest was just the rest.</b>
</i><br><br>There's a big secret Wes is keeping and I don't think I've ever cried this hard reading a book.<br>What he endures is gut wrenching!!<br>I cried plenty for him and for his dad.<br>They both have also suffered through tremendous loss.<br>Wes' mother died from illness and his younger brother committed suicide a year ago.<br><br>I have to mention one of the amazing secondary characters....Gabe.<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps27b220fc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431504i/865935._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps27b220fc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gabe well, he is by far, the BEST secondary character in any book I've ever read so far.<br>He'll have you laughing one minute, then bawling like a baby the next.<br>I adored this character and boy did he have me bawling like a baby!!<br>I did not expect those heart breaking words to come out of his mouth.<br><br><i>
  <b>"I would take your place. I just want you to know. If God told me that was penance for living the shitty life I've lived, I'd take your place. I asked Him, hell, I begged last night, and you know what? Nothing. Silence."</b>
</i><br><br>I could go on forever about why and how much I love this book.<br>All I'm going to say is that it's FABULOUS and I'd recommend it to everyone!!<br>Well done Rachel Van Dyken!!!!<br><br>FIVE+++++++++ to infinity stars!!!!!!!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1751659222676610843" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GlEOVJErVr6HkGR+SwM7vVYqrL2gDO5CmJDVQixEh6IjEv4qQRJxqSBbhZnE7VHogIvlkshlNldNkX04T4iKdg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UWrcrTY134hFresDY+3KhZAoQn/5Q52Mid717Eu0BGVoKSzT5gz4n+JmCuTsA6DQRokLUJEqRZlc312WKHgJsQ==')})
  }
//]]>
